  CODE
  {

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetPassword@1(NewPassword@1000 : Text);
    VAR
      ServicePassword@1001 : Record 1261;
    BEGIN
      IF ISNULLGUID("Password Key") OR NOT ServicePassword.GET("Password Key") THEN BEGIN
        ServicePassword.SavePassword(NewPassword);
        ServicePassword.INSERT(TRUE);
        "Password Key" := ServicePassword.Key;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ServicePassword.SavePassword(NewPassword);
        ServicePassword.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE GetPassword@3() : Text;
    VAR
      ServicePassword@1000 : Record 1261;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ISNULLGUID("Password Key") THEN
        IF ServicePassword.GET("Password Key") THEN
          EXIT(ServicePassword.GetPassword);
      EXIT('');
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE HasPassword@2() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(GetPassword <> '');
    END;

    PROCEDURE RemovePassword@4();
    VAR
      ServicePassword@1020 : Record 1261;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ISNULLGUID("Password Key") THEN BEGIN
        IF ServicePassword.GET("Password Key") THEN
          ServicePassword.DELETE(TRUE);

        CLEAR("Password Key");
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Pay Slip Integration - Development by Binesh                                                           |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
         PSI        11.21.18  Use this object for sending mail.
    }
    END.
  }
}

    [External]
    PROCEDURE AssistEdit@2() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      HumanResSetup.GET;
      HumanResSetup.TESTFIELD("Employee Nos.");
      IF NoSeriesMgt.SelectSeries(HumanResSetup."Employee Nos.",xRec."No. Series","No. Series") THEN BEGIN
        NoSeriesMgt.SetSeries("No.");
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE FullName@1() : Text[100];
    BEGIN
      IF "Middle Name" = '' THEN
        EXIT("First Name" + ' ' + "Last Name");

      EXIT("First Name" + ' ' + "Middle Name" + ' ' + "Last Name");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ValidateShortcutDimCode@29(FieldNumber@1000 : Integer;VAR ShortcutDimCode@1001 : Code[20]);
    BEGIN
      DimMgt.ValidateDimValueCode(FieldNumber,ShortcutDimCode);
      DimMgt.SaveDefaultDim(DATABASE::Employee,"No.",FieldNumber,ShortcutDimCode);
      MODIFY;
    END;

    [Internal]
    PROCEDURE DisplayMap@7();
    VAR
      MapPoint@1001 : Record 800;
      MapMgt@1000 : Codeunit 802;
    BEGIN
      IF MapPoint.FINDFIRST THEN
        MapMgt.MakeSelection(DATABASE::Employee,GETPOSITION)
      ELSE
        MESSAGE(Text000);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateSearchName@4();
    VAR
      PrevSearchName@1000 : Code[250];
    BEGIN
      PrevSearchName := xRec.FullName + ' ' + xRec.Initials;
      IF ((("First Name" <> xRec."First Name") OR ("Middle Name" <> xRec."Middle Name") OR ("Last Name" <> xRec."Last Name") OR
           (Initials <> xRec.Initials)) AND ("Search Name" = PrevSearchName))
      THEN
        "Search Name" := SetSearchNameToFullnameAndInitials;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetSearchNameToFullnameAndInitials@3() : Code[250];
    BEGIN
      EXIT(FullName + ' ' + Initials);
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE GetBankAccountNo@5() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF IBAN <> '' THEN
        EXIT(DELCHR(IBAN,'=<>'));

      IF "Bank Account No." <> '' THEN
        EXIT("Bank Account No.");
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE CheckBlockedEmployeeOnJnls@8(IsPosting@1000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      IF "Privacy Blocked" THEN BEGIN
        IF IsPosting THEN
          ERROR(BlockedEmplForJnrlPostingErr,"No.");
        ERROR(BlockedEmplForJnrlErr,"No.")
      END;
    END;

    }
    END.

    LOCAL PROCEDURE OpenBook@1000000020(FileNameP@1000000003 : Text;SheetNameP@1000000004 : Text);
    VAR
      i@1000000002 : Integer;
      EndOfLoop@1000000001 : Integer;
      Found@1000000000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF FileNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50001);

      IF NOT FileMgt.ClientFileExists(FileNameP) THEN
        ERROR(Text50003, FileName);

      IF SheetNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50002);
      IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
        XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
      XlApp.Visible(FALSE);// Set FALSE if you don't want to show.
      XlApp.Workbooks.Open(FileName,0,TRUE,6,Pwd,'',TRUE,1,'Chr(9)',TRUE,FALSE,0,TRUE,FALSE,0);
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;
      i := 1;
      EndOfLoop := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Count();
      WHILE (i <= EndOfLoop) AND (NOT Found) DO BEGIN
        XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(i);
        IF SheetNameP = XlWrkSht.Name THEN
          Found := TRUE;
        i += 1;
      END;
      IF Found THEN
        XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(SheetNameP)
      ELSE BEGIN
        QuitExcel;
        ERROR(Text50004,SheetNameP);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SelectSheetsName@6(FileNameP@1000 : Text) : Text[250];
    VAR
      SheetNames@1008 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Collections.ArrayList";
      SheetName@1002 : Text[250];
      SelectedSheetName@1007 : Text[250];
      SheetsList@1004 : Text[250];
      EndOfLoop@1003 : Integer;
      i@1001 : Integer;
      OptionNo@1005 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF FileNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50001);

      IF NOT FileMgt.ClientFileExists(FileNameP) THEN
        ERROR(Text50003, FileName);

      IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
        XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
      XlApp.Visible(FALSE);// Set FALSE if you don't want to show.
      XlApp.Workbooks.Open(FileName,0,TRUE,6,Pwd,'',TRUE,1,'Chr(9)',TRUE,FALSE,0,TRUE,FALSE,0);
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;
      i := 1;
      EndOfLoop := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Count();
      WHILE (i <= EndOfLoop) DO BEGIN
        XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(i);
        SheetName := XlWrkSht.Name;
        IF (SheetName <> '') AND (STRLEN(SheetsList) + STRLEN(SheetName) < 250) THEN
          SheetsList := SheetsList + SheetName + ','
        ELSE
          i := EndOfLoop;
        i := i + 1;
      END;
      QuitExcel;
      OptionNo := STRMENU(SheetsList,1);
      IF OptionNo <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(SELECTSTR(OptionNo,SheetsList))
      ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE QuitExcel@29();
    BEGIN
      // Clear the worksheet automation
      IF NOT ISNULL(XlWrkSht) THEN
        CLEAR(XlWrkSht);

      // Clear the workbook automation
      IF NOT ISNULL(XlWrkBk) THEN
        CLEAR(XlWrkBk);

      // Clear and quit the Excel application automation
      IF NOT ISNULL(XlApp) THEN BEGIN
        XlHelper.CallQuit(XlApp);
        CLEAR(XlApp);
      END;
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
</Code>

OBJECT Report 50043 Call Pay Slip
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=11/27/18;
    Time=[ 1:44:50 AM];
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=PSI;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    ProcessingOnly=Yes;
  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1000000000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               //OPen Book and get the LastCell Value
                               //OpenBook(FileName,SheetName);

                               IF EmpNo = '' THEN BEGIN
                                 PrintAllPaySlip := TRUE;
                                 SETFILTER(Number,'%1..%2',1,Loop);
                                 SpecificEmp_I_Value := 11;
                               END ELSE BEGIN
                                 CLEAR(PrintAllPaySlip);
                                 SETFILTER(Number,'%1..%2',1,1);
                                 SpecificEmp_I_Value -= 1;
                               END;
                               //CLoseExcel;
                               StepG:= SpecificEmp_I_Value;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  SpecificEmp_I_Value := StepG;
                                  SpecificEmp_I_Value += Number;
                                  IF EmpNo = '' THEN BEGIN
                                    OpenBook(FileName,SheetName);
                                    IF DELCHR(FORMAT(XlWrkSht.Range('C' + FORMAT(SpecificEmp_I_Value),'C' + FORMAT(SpecificEmp_I_Value)).Value),'<>',' ') = 'null' THEN
                                      CLEAR(EmpNo)
                                    ELSE
                                      EmpNo := DELCHR(FORMAT(XlWrkSht.Range('C' + FORMAT((SpecificEmp_I_Value)),'C' + FORMAT((SpecificEmp_I_Value))).Value),'<>',' ');
                                    CLoseExcel;
                                  END;

                                  Window.OPEN(Text001);
                                  PaySlipSetup.GET;
                                  AttachmentFileName := PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip File Path"+ EmpNo +('.pdf');
                                  IF FileMgt.ServerFileExists(AttachmentFileName) THEN
                                    FileMgt.DeleteServerFile(AttachmentFileName);
                                  CLEAR(PrintPaySlip);
                                  PrintPaySlip.Initialization(EmpNo,FileName,Pwd,SheetName,(SpecificEmp_I_Value),Month,Year);
                                  PrintPaySlip.USEREQUESTPAGE := FALSE;
                                  SetPRinter;
                                  PrinterSettings;
                                  Window.UPDATE(1, 'Printing PDF');
                                  PrintPaySlip.RUN;
                                  WaitOnPDF;
                                  FOR Cnt := 1 TO 5 DO
                                    IF NOT EXISTS(AttachmentFileName) THEN
                                      WaitWait;
                                  ResetPrinter;
                                  Window.CLOSE;

                                  IF PaySlipSetup."Email PDFs" THEN BEGIN
                                    PaySlipLedger.RESET;
                                    PaySlipLedger.SETRANGE("Emp No.",EmpNo);
                                    PaySlipLedger.SETRANGE(PaySlipLedger.Year,Year);
                                    PaySlipLedger.SETRANGE(PaySlipLedger.Month,FORMAT(Month));
                                    IF PaySlipLedger.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                      IF PaySlipLedger."Email Sent" THEN BEGIN
                                        IF CONFIRM('Already mail has sent, Do you want to send it again?',TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                                          IF TryCreateMail(AttachmentFileName) THEN BEGIN
                                            PaySlipLedger.Version := PaySlipLedger.Version + 1;
                                            PaySlipLedger."Sent Date":= CURRENTDATETIME;
                                            PaySlipLedger.MODIFY;
                                          END;
                                        END ELSE BEGIN
                                          DeletePDF(AttachmentFileName);
                                          EXIT;
                                        END;
                                        END ELSE BEGIN
                                          IF TryCreateMail(AttachmentFileName) THEN BEGIN
                                            PaySlipLedger."Email Sent":= TRUE;
                                            PaySlipLedger."Sent Date":= CURRENTDATETIME;
                                            PaySlipLedger.MODIFY;
                                            FileMgt.CopyClientFile(FileName,PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip History Path"+'Sent\PaySlip_'+FORMAT(Month)+FORMAT(Year)+'.xlsx',TRUE);
                                          END ELSE BEGIN
                                            PaySlipLedger."Email Sent":= FALSE;
                                            PaySlipLedger."Sent Date":= CURRENTDATETIME;
                                            PaySlipLedger.MODIFY;
                                            FileMgt.CopyClientFile(FileName,PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip History Path"+'ToSend\PaySlip_'+FORMAT(Month)+FORMAT(Year)+'.xlsx',TRUE);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF TryCreateMail(AttachmentFileName) THEN BEGIN
                                        PaySlipLedger.INIT;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Enytry No." := 0;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Emp No.":= EmpNo;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Year := Year;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Month:= FORMAT(Month);
                                        PaySlipLedger."Email Sent":= TRUE;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Sent Date":= CURRENTDATETIME;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Day := DATE2DMY(TODAY,1);
                                        PaySlipLedger.INSERT(TRUE);
                                        IF PaySlipSetup."Move Excel File after Emailing" THEN
                                          FileMgt.CopyClientFile(FileName,PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip History Path"+'Sent\PaySlip_'+FORMAT(Month)+FORMAT(Year)+'.xlsx',TRUE);
                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                        PaySlipLedger.INIT;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Enytry No." := 0;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Emp No.":= EmpNo;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Year := Year;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Month:= FORMAT(Month);
                                        PaySlipLedger."Email Sent":= FALSE;
                                        PaySlipLedger."Sent Date":= CURRENTDATETIME;
                                        PaySlipLedger.Day := DATE2DMY(TODAY,1);
                                        PaySlipLedger.INSERT(TRUE);
                                        IF PaySlipSetup."Move Excel File after Emailing" THEN
                                          FileMgt.CopyClientFile(FileName,PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip History Path"+'ToSend\PaySlip_'+FORMAT(Month)+FORMAT(Year)+'.xlsx',TRUE);
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF PaySlipSetup."Move PDFs after Emailing" THEN BEGIN
                                    ClientFileName := PaySlipSetup."Payment Slip History Path"+EmpNo+'.pdf';
                                    FileMgt.CopyClientFile(AttachmentFileName,ClientFileName,TRUE);
                                  END;

                                  IF PaySlipSetup."Delete PDFs after Emailing" THEN
                                    DeletePDF(AttachmentFileName);

                                  CLEAR(EmpNo);
                                END;
                                 }

  }
  REQUESTPAGE
  {
    PROPERTIES
    {
      OnOpenPage=BEGIN
                   IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2018 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2018"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2019 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2019"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2020 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2020"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2021 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2021"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2022 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2022"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2023 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2023"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2024 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2024"
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,3) = 2025 THEN
                     Year := Year::"2025";

                   IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 1 THEN
                     Month := Month::January
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 2 THEN
                     Month := Month::February
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 3 THEN
                     Month := Month::March
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 4 THEN
                     Month := Month::April
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 5 THEN
                     Month := Month::May
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 6 THEN
                     Month := Month::June
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 7 THEN
                     Month := Month::July
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 8 THEN
                     Month := Month::August
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 9 THEN
                     Month := Month::September
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 10 THEN
                     Month := Month::October
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 11 THEN
                     Month := Month::November
                   ELSE IF DATE2DMY(TODAY,2) = 12 THEN
                     Month := Month::December;
                 END;

    }
    CONTROLS
    {
      { 1000000006;;Container;
                  Name=option;
                  ContainerType=ContentArea }

      { 1000000005;1;Group  ;
                  Name=General;
                  GroupType=Group }

      { 1000000003;2;Field  ;
                  Name=Year;
                  SourceExpr=Year }

      { 1000000007;2;Field  ;
                  Name=Month;
                  SourceExpr=Month }

      { 1000000004;2;Field  ;
                  Name=Emp No.;
                  SourceExpr=EmpNo }

      { 1000000002;2;Field  ;
                  Name=FileName;
                  SourceExpr=FileName;
                  OnLookup=BEGIN
                             FileName := FileMgt.OpenFileDialog(Text50006,'',Excel2007FileType);
                           END;
                            }

      { 1000000001;2;Field  ;
                  Name=Password;
                  ExtendedDatatype=Masked;
                  SourceExpr=Pwd }

      { 1000000000;2;Field  ;
                  Name=SheetName;
                  SourceExpr=SheetName;
                  OnValidate=BEGIN
                               IF FileName = '' THEN
                                 ERROR(Text50001);
                             END;

                  OnLookup=BEGIN
                             IF NOT FileMgt.ClientFileExists(FileName) THEN
                               ERROR(Text50003, FileName);

                             IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
                               XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
                             XlApp.Visible(FALSE);// Set FALSE if you don't want to show.
                             XlApp.Workbooks.Open(FileName,0,TRUE,6,Pwd,'',TRUE,1,'Chr(9)',TRUE,FALSE,0,TRUE,FALSE,0);
                             XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;
                             XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(1);
                             SheetName := XlWrkSht.Name;
                             XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(SheetName);

                             Maxi := XlWrkSht.Cells.SpecialCells(11,2).Row; //Finding Last RowNo---/ICS--->>//35
                             Maxj := XlWrkSht.Cells.SpecialCells(11,2).Column; //last coloumn no.
                             IValue:= 12;
                             LastCellValue := (Maxi - 6);//35-6=29
                             Loop := LastCellValue -  IValue;//29-12=17
                             //Search the EmpNo and get the I value := SpecificEmp_I_Value
                             REPEAT
                               IF FORMAT(XlWrkSht.Range('C' + FORMAT(IValue),'C' + FORMAT(IValue)).Value) = EmpNo THEN
                                 SpecificEmp_I_Value := IValue;
                               IValue += 1;
                             UNTIL IValue > Maxi;
                             QuitExcel;
                           END;
                            }

    }
  }
  LABELS
  {
  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      EmpNo@1000000000 : Code[20];
      FileName@1000000001 : Text;
      Pwd@1000000002 : Text;
      SheetName@1000000003 : Text;
      FileMgt@1000000004 : Codeunit 419;
      XlApp@1000000009 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel, Version=15.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=71e9bce111e9429c'.Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.ApplicationClass" RUNONCLIENT;
      XlWrkBk@1000000008 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel, Version=15.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=71e9bce111e9429c'.Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Workbook" RUNONCLIENT;
      XlWrkSht@1000000007 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel, Version=15.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=71e9bce111e9429c'.Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Worksheet" RUNONCLIENT;
      Text50000@1000000020 : TextConst 'ENU=Excel not found.;ESM=No encontr¢ Excel.;FRC=Programme Excel non trouvÇ.;ENC=Excel not found.';
      Text50001@1000000019 : TextConst 'ENU=You must enter a file name.;ESM=Debe introd. nombre fichero;FRC=Vous devez saisir un nom de fichier.;ENC=You must enter a file name.';
      Text50002@1000000018 : TextConst 'ENU=You must enter an Excel worksheet name.;ESM=Debe introducir un nombre hoja Excel.;FRC=Vous devez saisir un nom de feuille Excel.;ENC=You must enter an Excel worksheet name.';

    PROCEDURE SelectSheetsName@6(FileNameP@1000 : Text) : Text[250];
    VAR
      SheetNames@1008 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Collections.ArrayList";
      SheetName@1002 : Text[250];
      SelectedSheetName@1007 : Text[250];
      SheetsList@1004 : Text[250];
      EndOfLoop@1003 : Integer;
      i@1001 : Integer;
      OptionNo@1005 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF FileNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50001);

      IF NOT FileMgt.ClientFileExists(FileNameP) THEN
        ERROR(Text50003, FileName);

      IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
        XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
      XlApp.Visible(FALSE);
      XlApp.Workbooks.Open(FileName,0,TRUE,6,Pwd,'',TRUE,1,'Chr(9)',TRUE,FALSE,0,TRUE,FALSE,0);
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;
      XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(1);
      SheetName := XlWrkSht.Name;
      XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(SheetName);

      Maxi := XlWrkSht.Cells.SpecialCells(11,2).Row;
      Maxj := XlWrkSht.Cells.SpecialCells(11,2).Column;
      IValue:= 12;
      LastCellValue := (Maxi - 6);
      Loop := LastCellValue -  IValue;
      REPEAT
        IF FORMAT(XlWrkSht.Range('C' + FORMAT(IValue),'C' + FORMAT(IValue)).Value) = EmpNo THEN
          SpecificEmp_I_Value := IValue;
        IValue += 1;
      UNTIL IValue > Maxi;
      QuitExcel;
    END;

    PROCEDURE QuitExcel@29();
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ISNULL(XlWrkSht) THEN
        CLEAR(XlWrkSht);

      IF NOT ISNULL(XlWrkBk) THEN
        CLEAR(XlWrkBk);

      IF NOT ISNULL(XlApp) THEN BEGIN
        XlHelper.CallQuit(XlApp);
        CLEAR(XlApp);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CLoseExcel@1000000005();
    BEGIN
      XlWrkBk.Close(FALSE,FileName,TRUE);
      XlApp.Quit;
      CLEAR(XlApp);
    END;

    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE OpenBook@1000000020(FileNameP@1000000003 : Text;SheetNameP@1000000004 : Text);
    VAR
      i@1000000002 : Integer;
      EndOfLoop@1000000001 : Integer;
      Found@1000000000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF FileNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50001);

      IF NOT FileMgt.ClientFileExists(FileNameP) THEN
        ERROR(Text50003, FileName);

      IF SheetNameP = '' THEN
        ERROR(Text50002);
      IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
        XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
      XlApp.Visible(FALSE);
      XlApp.Workbooks.Open(FileName,0,TRUE,6,Pwd,'',TRUE,1,'Chr(9)',TRUE,FALSE,0,TRUE,FALSE,0);
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;
      i := 1;
      EndOfLoop := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Count();
      WHILE (i <= EndOfLoop) AND (NOT Found) DO BEGIN
        XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(i);
        IF SheetNameP = XlWrkSht.Name THEN
          Found := TRUE;
        i += 1;
      END;
      IF Found THEN
        XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(SheetNameP)
      ELSE BEGIN
        QuitExcel;
        ERROR(Text50004,SheetNameP);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE TryCreateMail@1000000000(AttachmentFile@1000000002 : Text);
    VAR
      SMTPMailSetup@1000000015 : Record 409;
      SmtpClient@1000000013 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.SmtpClient";
      MailMessage@1000000012 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailMessage";
      MailCredintials@1000000011 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.NetworkCredential";
      MailAddress@1000000010 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailAddress";
      MailAddressFrom@1000000009 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailAddress";
      MailAddressCollectionTo@1000000008 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailAddressCollection";
      MailAddressCollectionCC@1000000007 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailAddressCollection";
      MailAddressCollectionBCC@1000000006 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.MailAddressCollection";
      MailAttachments@1000000005 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.AttachmentCollection";
      MailAttachment@1000000004 : DotNet "'System, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.Mail.Attachment";
      Cr@1000000003 : Char;
    BEGIN
      EmployeeG.GET(EmpNo);
      SMTPMailSetup.GET;
      SMTPMailSetup.TESTFIELD("SMTP Server");
      SMTPMailSetup.TESTFIELD("User ID");
      MailMessage := MailMessage.MailMessage;
      MailMessage.Subject := STRSUBSTNO('Pay slip for the month of '+ FORMAT(Month) + ' ' + FORMAT(Year));
      MailMessage.Body := STRSUBSTNO('Dear '+ EmployeeG.FullName + ',');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('<br><br>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('Please find the attached PaySlip for the Month of '+ FORMAT(Month) + ' ' + FORMAT(Year)+'.');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('<br><br>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('Sincerely,');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('<br>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('Accounting Officer');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('<br>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('ICS Technology Services Pvt Ltd.');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('<br><br>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+FORMAT(Cr)+STRSUBSTNO('<hr>');
      MailMessage.Body := MailMessage.Body+STRSUBSTNO('This is a system generated mail. Please do not reply to this Mail ID.');

      MailAttachments := MailMessage.Attachments;
      MailAttachment := MailAttachment.Attachment(AttachmentFile);
      MailAttachments.Add(MailAttachment);

      MailMessage.IsBodyHtml := TRUE;

      MailAddress := MailAddress.MailAddress(SMTPMailSetup."User ID");
      MailAddressFrom := MailMessage.From(MailAddress);

      MailAddressCollectionTo := MailMessage."To";
      MailAddressCollectionTo.Add(EmployeeG."E-Mail");

      MailCredintials := MailCredintials.NetworkCredential(SMTPMailSetup."User ID",SMTPMailSetup.GetPassword);
      SmtpClient := SmtpClient.SmtpClient();
      SmtpClient.Host := SMTPMailSetup."SMTP Server";
      SmtpClient.Port := SMTPMailSetup."SMTP Server Port";
      SmtpClient.EnableSsl := SMTPMailSetup."Secure Connection";
      SmtpClient.UseDefaultCredentials := FALSE;
      SmtpClient.Credentials := MailCredintials;
      SmtpClient.Send(MailMessage);
    END;

    PROCEDURE PrinterSettings@1100785003();
    VAR
      EmployeeL@1000000000 : Record 5200;
      PrinterSelection@1000000001 : Record 78;
    BEGIN
      PrinterSelection.GET(USERID,50042);
      PrinterSelection.TESTFIELD("Printer Name");
      BullZipPDF.printerName := PrinterSelection."Printer Name";
      RunOnceFile := BullZipPDF.GetSettingsFilePath(TRUE);
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('Output', AttachmentFileName);
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('Showsettings', 'Never');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('ShowPDF', 'No');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('ShowProgress', 'No');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('ShowProgressFinished', 'No');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('SuppressErrors', 'Yes');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('ConfirmOverwrite', 'No');
      EmployeeL.GET(EmpNo);
      //>>Add Password
      EmployeeL.TESTFIELD("Pay Slip Password");
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('OwnerPassword', PaySlipSetup."Master Password");
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('UserPassword', EmployeeL."Pay Slip Password");
      //<<Add Password

      //>>Sign with a digital certificate.
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('SignCertificate', PaySlipSetup."eSign Certificate Path");
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('SignPassword', PaySlipSetup."eSign Password");
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('ShowSignature', 'yes');
      //<<Sign with a digital certificate.

      //>>Add watermark
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkText', 'https://sbinesh.blogspot.com/');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkColor', '#FF0000');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkVerticalPosition', 'top');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkHorizontalPosition', 'right');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkRotation', '90');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkOutlineWidth', '0.5');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkFontSize', '20');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkVerticalAdjustment', '5');
      BullZipPDF.SetValue('WatermarkHorizontalAdjustment', '1');
      //<<Add watermark
      BullZipPDF.WriteSettings(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE WaitOnPDF@1100785004();
    BEGIN
      TimeOut := 0;
      WHILE EXISTS(RunOnceFile) AND (TimeOut < 10) DO BEGIN
        Window.UPDATE(1, 'Waiting... - ' + FORMAT(TimeOut));
        SLEEP(500);
        TimeOut := TimeOut + 1;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE WaitWait@1100785007();
    BEGIN
      TimeOut := 0;
      WHILE TimeOut < PaySlipSetup."PDF Write Delay (seconds)" DO BEGIN
        Window.UPDATE(1, 'Waiting - ' + FORMAT(Cnt) + ' - ' + FORMAT(TimeOut));
        SLEEP(500);
        TimeOut := TimeOut + 1;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeletePDF@1100785009(xFileName@1100785001 : Text);
    BEGIN
      Window.OPEN('Deleting File...');
      IF FileMgt.ServerFileExists(xFileName) THEN
        FileMgt.DeleteServerFile(xFileName);
      Window.CLOSE;
    END;
